  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;

  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);

  chops-button, a.button, .button {

  a.button, .button {

  }

    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);

  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

  .medium-heading {

          --mr-toggled-font-family: inherit;
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-open-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[issueClosed] {
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: nowrap;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          background: var(--monorail-metadata-toggled-bg);
          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);
          border-bottom: var(--chops-normal-border);
          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }
        mr-issue-details {
          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;
          padding-left: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);
          padding-left: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          width: 50%;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;
        }
        @media (max-width: 1126px) {
          .container-issue-content {
            flex-direction: column;
            padding: 0 var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 0;
            border: 0;
          }
        }
        @media (max-width: 840px) {
          .container-outside {

          .metadata-container {

            position: static;
          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

& Many vulnerabilities in command injection were found (attached bellow) , using different payloads .



<span class="line"><!---->&amp; Many vulnerabilities in command injection were found (attached bellow) , using different payloads .<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





#### Please briefly explain who can exploit the vulnerability, and what they gain when doing so



<span class="line"><!---->#### Please briefly explain who can exploit the vulnerability, and what they gain when doing so<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**Vulnerability Type: Command Injection**



<span class="line"><!---->**Vulnerability Type: Command Injection**<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**Description:** The application is vulnerable to command injection, which allows attackers to execute arbitrary commands on the server. An attacker can exploit this vulnerability by injecting a command via an application parameter that will be executed by the application with the privileges of the user running the application.



<span class="line"><!---->**Description:** The application is vulnerable to command injection, which allows attackers to execute arbitrary commands on the server. An attacker can exploit this vulnerability by injecting a command via an application parameter that will be executed by the application with the privileges of the user running the application.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**Proof of Concept:**



<span class="line"><!---->**Proof of Concept:**<!----></span>



<br>





**For the  Payload: 127.0.0.1; cat /etc/shadow (The PoC may differs from payload to payload for that I am attaching list of payloads used  )**



<span class="line"><!---->**For the  Payload: 127.0.0.1; cat /etc/shadow (The PoC may differs from payload to payload for that I am attaching list of payloads used  )**<!----></span>



<br>





Identify the vulnerable input field in the application that accepts user input.



<span class="line"><!---->Identify the vulnerable input field in the application that accepts user input.<!----></span>



<br>





Enter the following payload in the input field:



<span class="line"><!---->Enter the following payload in the input field:<!----></span>



<br>





 127.0.0.1; cat /etc/shadow



<span class="line"><!----> 127.0.0.1; cat /etc/shadow<!----></span>



<br>





Submit the input.



<span class="line"><!---->Submit the input.<!----></span>



<br>





The application will execute the injected command, which will attempt to display the contents of the /etc/shadow file.



<span class="line"><!---->The application will execute the injected command, which will attempt to display the contents of the /etc/shadow file.<!----></span>



<br>





If the application has sufficient privileges to execute the command, it will return the contents of the /etc/shadow file in the response.



<span class="line"><!---->If the application has sufficient privileges to execute the command, it will return the contents of the /etc/shadow file in the response.<!----></span>



<br>





The attacker can then extract the sensitive information from the response, such as user passwords, and use it to gain unauthorized access to the system.



<span class="line"><!---->The attacker can then extract the sensitive information from the response, such as user passwords, and use it to gain unauthorized access to the system.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





**Steps to reproduce:**



<span class="line"><!---->**Steps to reproduce:**<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Send a request with the payload to the vulnerable parameter.



<span class="line"><!---->Send a request with the payload to the vulnerable parameter.<!----></span>



<br>





The application will execute the injected command.



<span class="line"><!---->The application will execute the injected command.<!----></span>



<br>





The response will contain the contents of the /etc/shadow file.



<span class="line"><!---->The response will contain the contents of the /etc/shadow file.<!----></span>



<br>





Who can exploit the vulnerability: An attacker with access to the vulnerable parameter in the application can exploit this vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->Who can exploit the vulnerability: An attacker with access to the vulnerable parameter in the application can exploit this vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>





Impact of the vulnerability: An attacker can execute arbitrary commands on the server and gain access to sensitive information, modify or delete data, and even take control of the server.



<span class="line"><!---->Impact of the vulnerability: An attacker can execute arbitrary commands on the server and gain access to sensitive information, modify or delete data, and even take control of the server.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**Mitigation:**



<span class="line"><!---->**Mitigation:**<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Validate user input to ensure that it does not contain any command injection payloads.



<span class="line"><!---->Validate user input to ensure that it does not contain any command injection payloads.<!----></span>



<br>





Use parameterized queries or prepared statements to avoid command injection vulnerabilities.



<span class="line"><!---->Use parameterized queries or prepared statements to avoid command injection vulnerabilities.<!----></span>



<br>





Use a sandboxed environment to execute user-supplied input.



<span class="line"><!---->Use a sandboxed environment to execute user-supplied input.<!----></span>



<br>





Limit the privileges of the user running the application to the minimum necessary to perform its function.



<span class="line"><!---->Limit the privileges of the user running the application to the minimum necessary to perform its function.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





**For more information I am attaching all the files regarding to this bug , please check it out .**



<span class="line"><!---->**For more information I am attaching all the files regarding to this bug , please check it out .**<!----></span>

          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
